SELECT COUNT(*) FROM Patient AS T1 INNER JOIN Laboratory AS T2 ON T1.`ID` = T2.`ID` WHERE T1.`Admission` = '-' AND T2.`ALP` < 300

SELECT T1.`ID` FROM Examination AS T1 INNER JOIN Laboratory AS T2 ON T1.`ID` = T2.`ID` WHERE T2.`CRE` < 1.5 AND T1.`aCL IgA` = (SELECT MAX(`aCL IgA`) FROM Examination)

SELECT T2.`Date` FROM customers AS T1 INNER JOIN yearmonth AS T2 ON T1.`CustomerID` = T2.`CustomerID` WHERE T1.`Segment` = 'SME' AND T2.`Date` BETWEEN '201301' AND '201312' ORDER BY T2.`Consumption` DESC LIMIT 1
WITH CTE AS (   SELECT      c.`Segment`,     MIN(y.`Consumption`) AS min_consumption   FROM      customers c   INNER JOIN      yearmonth y ON c.`CustomerID` = y.`CustomerID`   WHERE      c.`Currency` = 'CZK'     AND y.`Date` BETWEEN '201301' AND '201312'   GROUP BY      c.`Segment`   HAVING      c.`Segment` IN ('SME', 'LAM', 'KAM') ) SELECT    (SELECT min_consumption FROM CTE WHERE `Segment` = 'SME') - (SELECT min_consumption FROM CTE WHERE `Segment` = 'LAM') AS SME_LAM_diff,   (SELECT min_consumption FROM CTE WHERE `Segment` = 'LAM') - (SELECT min_consumption FROM CTE WHERE `Segment` = 'KAM') AS LAM_KAM_diff,   (SELECT min_consumption FROM CTE WHERE `Segment` = 'KAM') - (SELECT min_consumption FROM CTE WHERE `Segment` = 'SME') AS KAM_SME_diff
SELECT Segment FROM (SELECT c.Segment, (SUM(CASE WHEN substr(ym.Date, 1, 4) = '2013' THEN ym.Consumption ELSE 0 END) - SUM(CASE WHEN substr(ym.Date, 1, 4) = '2012' THEN ym.Consumption ELSE 0 END)) / SUM(CASE WHEN substr(ym.Date, 1, 4) = '2013' THEN ym.Consumption ELSE 0 END) * 100 AS pct_increase FROM customers c INNER JOIN yearmonth ym ON c.CustomerID = ym.CustomerID WHERE c.Currency = 'EUR' AND c.Segment IN ('SME', 'LAM', 'KAM') GROUP BY c.Segment ORDER BY pct_increase DESC LIMIT 1) UNION ALL SELECT Segment FROM (SELECT c.Segment, (SUM(CASE WHEN substr(ym.Date, 1, 4) = '2013' THEN ym.Consumption ELSE 0 END) - SUM(CASE WHEN substr(ym.Date, 1, 4) = '2012' THEN ym.Consumption ELSE 0 END)) / SUM(CASE WHEN substr(ym.Date, 1, 4) = '2013' THEN ym.Consumption ELSE 0 END) * 100 AS pct_increase FROM customers c INNER JOIN yearmonth ym ON c.CustomerID = ym.CustomerID WHERE c.Currency = 'EUR' AND c.Segment IN ('SME', 'LAM', 'KAM') GROUP BY c.Segment ORDER BY pct_increase ASC LIMIT 1)

SELECT T1.`Currency` FROM customers AS T1 INNER JOIN yearmonth AS T2 ON T1.`CustomerID` = T2.`CustomerID` WHERE T2.`Consumption` = 214582.17 AND T2.`Date` = '201306'
SELECT DISTINCT T3.Country FROM customers AS T1 INNER JOIN transactions_1k AS T2 ON T1.CustomerID = T2.CardID INNER JOIN gasstations AS T3 ON T2.GasStationID = T3.GasStationID WHERE T2.CardID = 667467
SELECT NULL FROM transactions_1k AS T1 INNER JOIN customers AS T2 ON T1.`CustomerID` = T2.`CustomerID` WHERE T1.`Amount` = 548.4 AND T1.`Date` = '2012-08-24'
SELECT CAST(SUM(IIF(T1.`Currency` = 'EUR', 1, 0)) AS REAL) * 100 / COUNT(T1.`CustomerID`) FROM `customers` AS T1 INNER JOIN `transactions_1k` AS T2 ON T1.`CustomerID` = T2.`CustomerID` WHERE T2.`Date` = '2012-08-25'
SELECT (T2.consumption_2012 - T2.consumption_2013) * 1.0 / T2.consumption_2012 FROM (SELECT T1.`CustomerID`, SUM(CASE WHEN T1.`Date` LIKE '2012%' THEN T1.`Consumption` ELSE 0 END) AS consumption_2012, SUM(CASE WHEN T1.`Date` LIKE '2013%' THEN T1.`Consumption` ELSE 0 END) AS consumption_2013 FROM yearmonth AS T1 INNER JOIN transactions_1k AS T2 ON T1.`CustomerID` = T2.`CustomerID` WHERE T2.`Date` = '2012-08-25' AND T2.`Amount` = 634.8 GROUP BY T1.`CustomerID`) AS T2
SELECT T1.GasStationID FROM `transactions_1k` AS T1 INNER JOIN `gasstations` AS T2 ON T1.GasStationID = T2.GasStationID GROUP BY T1.GasStationID ORDER BY SUM(T1.Amount * T1.Price) DESC LIMIT 1
SELECT CAST(SUM(IIF(`Segment` = 'Premium', 1, 0)) AS REAL) * 100 / COUNT(*) FROM gasstations WHERE `Country` = 'SVK'
SELECT SUM(T1.`Amount`) FROM transactions_1k AS T1 WHERE T1.`CustomerID` = 38508 AND SUBSTR(T1.`Date`, 1, 7) = '2012-01'
SELECT p.`Description` FROM products AS p INNER JOIN transactions_1k AS t ON p.`ProductID` = t.`ProductID` GROUP BY p.`Description` ORDER BY SUM(t.`Amount`) DESC LIMIT 5
SELECT T1.`CustomerID`, SUM(T2.`Amount` * T2.`Price`) AS TotalSpent, SUM(T2.`Price` * T2.`Amount`) / SUM(T2.`Amount`) AS AvgPricePerItem, T1.`Currency` FROM customers AS T1 INNER JOIN transactions_1k AS T2 ON T1.`CustomerID` = T2.`CustomerID` GROUP BY T1.`CustomerID` ORDER BY TotalSpent DESC LIMIT 1
SELECT T1.`Country` FROM `gasstations` AS T1 INNER JOIN `transactions_1k` AS T2 ON T1.`GasStationID` = T2.`GasStationID` WHERE T2.`ProductID` = 2 ORDER BY T2.`Price` DESC LIMIT 1
SELECT DISTINCT y.`Consumption` FROM transactions_1k AS t INNER JOIN yearmonth AS y ON t.`CustomerID` = y.`CustomerID` WHERE t.`Price` / t.`Amount` > 29.00 AND t.`ProductID` = 5 AND y.`Date` = '201208'
